\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \ \ \ \ PetscReal\ sigma\ =\ window/3.0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \ \ \ \ PetscReal\ sum\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \ \ \ \ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Create\ Gaussian\ kernel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(PetscInt\ i=0;\ i<window;\ i++)\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00296\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ output[i]\ =\ 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{00298\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00299\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ PetscInt\ idx\ =\ i\ +\ j;}

\DoxyCodeLine{00555\ \ \ \ \ \ \ r\ =\ -\/PI*PI/6\ +\ l*(0.5*l\ -\/\ log(-\/x));}
\DoxyCodeLine{00556\ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ =\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00557\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ ==\ -\/1)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00558\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ -\/PI*PI/12;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00559\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ <\ 0)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00560\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ PetscReal\ l\ =\ log1p(-\/x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00561\ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ x/(x\ -\/\ 1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00562\ \ \ \ \ \ \ r\ =\ -\/0.5*l*l;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00563\ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ =\ -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00564\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ ==\ 0)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00565\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00566\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ <\ 0.5)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00567\ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00568\ \ \ \ \ \ \ r\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00569\ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ =\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00570\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ <\ 1)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00571\ \ \ \ \ \ \ y\ =\ 1\ -\/\ x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00572\ \ \ \ \ \ \ r\ =\ PI*PI/6\ -\/\ log(x)*log1p(-\/x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00573\ \ \ \ \ \ \ s\ =\ -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00574\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ ==\ 1)\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{00576\ \ \ \ \ \}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (x\ <\ 2)\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{00812\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00815\ \ \ \ \ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{00816\ \ \ \ \ sqrt}

\DoxyCodeLine{00818\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ axis.x\ *\ axis.x\ +}
\DoxyCodeLine{00819\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ axis.y\ *\ axis.y\ +}

\DoxyCodeLine{00826\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ sprintf(error,\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}provided\ rotation\ axis\ too\ small\ to\ working\ precision\(\backslash\)n"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{00827\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{io_8h_a68cb6557f006e2a0740834acd0d4e4db}{fatalErrorInFunction}}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}nRot"{}},\ \ error);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00828\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00829\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00830\ \ \ \ \ axis.x\ =\ axis.x\ /\ axisMag;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00831\ \ \ \ \ axis.y\ =\ axis.y\ /\ axisMag;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00832\ \ \ \ \ axis.z\ =\ axis.z\ /\ axisMag;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00833\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00834\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ compute\ sine\ and\ cosine}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00835\ \ \ \ \ costheta\ =\ cos(theta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00836\ \ \ \ \ sintheta\ =\ sin(theta);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00837\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00838\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ explicitly\ compute\ rotation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00839\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.x\ +=\ (costheta\ +\ (1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.x\ *\ axis.x\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )\ *\ vStart.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00840\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.x\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.x\ *\ axis.y\ -\/\ axis.z\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00841\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.x\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.x\ *\ axis.z\ +\ axis.y\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00842\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00843\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.y\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.x\ *\ axis.y\ +\ axis.z\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00844\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.y\ +=\ (costheta\ +\ (1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.y\ *\ axis.y\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )\ *\ vStart.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00845\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.y\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.y\ *\ axis.z\ -\/\ axis.x\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00846\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00847\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.z\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.x\ *\ axis.z\ -\/\ axis.y\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00848\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.z\ +=\ ((1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.y\ *\ axis.z\ +\ axis.x\ *\ sintheta)\ *\ vStart.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{00849\ \ \ \ \ vRotated.z\ +=\ (costheta\ +\ (1\ -\/\ costheta)\ *\ axis.z\ *\ axis.z\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ )\ *\ vStart.z;}

\DoxyCodeLine{05873\ \textcolor{keyword}{inline}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ findInterpolationWeights(PetscReal\ *weights,\ PetscInt\ *labels,\ PetscReal\ *pvec,\ PetscInt\ npts,\ PetscReal\ pval)}
\DoxyCodeLine{05874\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{05875\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ equality\ tolerance:\ if\ equal\ data\ points\ up\ to\ re-\/tol\ =\ 1e-\/5\ are\ found,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05876\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ that\ interpolation\ point\ is\ skipped\ because\ it\ does\ not\ provide\ information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05877\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ would\ result\ in\ a\ division\ by\ zero\ when\ computing\ the\ weights.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{05882\ \ \ \ \ PetscReal\ eps\ =\ (pvec[npts-\/1]\ -\/\ pvec[0])\ /\ npts;}

\DoxyCodeLine{05885\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ char\ error[512];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05886\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ sprintf(error,\ "{}query\ point\ \%lf\ outside\ of\ bounds\ [\%lf\ -\/\ \%lf]...\ was\ told\ not\ to\ extrapolate\(\backslash\)n"{},\ pval,\ pvec[0]-\/eps,\ pvec[npts-\/1]+eps);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05887\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ fatalErrorInFunction("{}findInterpolationWeights"{},\ \ error);}}
